1d:T681,The Forgers goes on a winter vacation, changes the course of the world's fate, and Loid Forger makes an exciting return to threezero's FigZero 1/6 scale figure series, with a brand-new winter costume as seen in the movie SPY×FAMILY CODE: White!
FigZero 1/6 Loid Forger (Winter Costume Ver.) is approximately 12" (31.2 cm) tall, and is a fully-articulated collectible figure made of ABS, PVC, and POM plastics with approximately 32 points of articulation and fabric textiles. The detailed sculpts and tailored outfits bring the anime character to life.
FigZero 1/6 Loid Forger (Winter Costume Ver.)'s costume features the outfit he wears in the movie, SPY×FAMILY CODE: White, which includes a white shirt, brown coat, brown scarf, pants, and shoes. Additionally, the costume comes with his glasses and wristwatch. Other accessories include a pistol, two interchangeable faceplates (one with a default expression and one with a smiling face), as well as three pairs of interchangeable hands to create dynamic action poses.

FEATURES

- Approximately 12" (~31.2cm) tall
- Approximately 32 points of articulation
- Costume made of a combination of fabric and plastic parts
- Various accessories provided for different poses

COSTUME

- One (1) pc of Brown Coat
- One (1) pc of Brown Scarf
- One (1) pair of Black Pants
- One (1) pair of Brown Shoes
- One (1) pc of Wristwatch
- One (1) pc of Glasses

ACCESSORIES

- One (1) pc of pistol
- Two (2) interchangeable faceplates: one (1) face with the default expression, and one (1) smiling face
- Three (3) pairs of gloved interchangeable hands: relaxed hands, pistol-holding hands, and fists1e:T643,threezero's SPY×FAMILY 1/6 scale figure series falls under the FigZero product line, known for its highly-poseable anime figures with detailed sculpts and tailored outfits that bring to life the recognizable character designs as seen in the beloved anime series.

FigZero 1/6 Yor Forger is approximately 11.2" (28.5 cm) tall, and is a fully-articulated 1/6-scale collectible figure made of ABS, PVC, and POM plastics with 35 points of articulation and fabric textiles.
Various accessories are provided for different exciting poses! FigZero 1/6 Yor Forger comes with a total of three interchangeable faceplates (one default expression, one action expression, and one serious expression). The character's costume includes Yor's iconic form-fitting halter-style black dress and a pair of black thigh-high boots, made of fabric and plastic materials. Other accessories included are four sets of interchangeable hands in different positions and a pair of needle awls for recreating action poses.

- Approximately 11.2" (~28.5cm) tall

- Costume made of a combination of fabric and plastic parts
